#			--------------------------------------------------------------- book 0 is selected
w 30 00 00 
w 30 7f 00 
#			--------------------------------------------------------------- page 1 is selected
w 30 00 01 
#			# reg[  0][  1][  1] = 0x00	; Disable weak AVDD to DVDD connection
w 30 01 00 
#			# reg[  0][  1][121] = 0x33	; MicPGA Quick Charge = 1.1/0.5 ms
w 30 79 33 
#			# reg[  0][  1][122] = 0x01	; Set the REF charging time to 30ms
w 30 7a 01 
#			# reg[  0][  1][ 33] = 0x28	; CP Clock Divider = 4 (8MHz/(6*4)) = 333kHz
w 30 21 28 
#			# reg[  0][  1][ 34] = 0x33	; Buffered AVSS_SENSE, 1x current, DC offset
w 30 22 33 
#			# reg[  0][  1][ 35] = 0x30	; CP Auto-power enabled, Dynamic offset corr.
w 30 23 30 
#			--------------------------------------------------------------- page 0 is selected
w 30 00 00 
#			# reg[  0][  0][  4] = 0x33	; DAC_CLKIN / ADC_CLKIN = PLL_CLK
w 30 04 33 
#			# reg[  0][  0][  5] = 0x00	; PLL_CLKIN = MCLK1, PLL low range
w 30 05 00 
#			# reg[  0][  0][  6] = 0x91	; PLL on, P=1, R=1
w 30 06 91 
#			# reg[  0][  0][  8] = 0x00	; D = 0000 (MSB)
w 30 08 00 
#			# reg[  0][  0][  9] = 0x00	; D = 0000 (LSB)
w 30 09 00 
#			# reg[  0][  0][  7] = 0x08	; J=8
w 30 07 08 
#			# reg[  0][  0][ 13] = 0x01	; DOSR = 384 (MSB)
w 30 0d 01 
#			# reg[  0][  0][ 14] = 0x80	; DOSR = 384 (LSB)
w 30 0e 80 
#			# reg[  0][  0][ 18] = 0x02	; NADC = 2, divider powered off
w 30 12 02 
#			# reg[  0][  0][ 19] = 0x98	; MADC = 24, divider powered on
w 30 13 98 
#			# reg[  0][  0][ 20] = 0x80	; AOSR = 128
w 30 14 80 
#			# reg[  0][  0][ 12] = 0x88	; MDAC = 8, divider powered on
w 30 0c 88 
#			# reg[  0][  0][ 11] = 0x82	; NDAC = 2, divider powered off; NDAC = 2, divider powered on
w 30 0b 82 
#			# reg[0][0][82] = 0
w 30 52 00 
#			# reg[0][0][83] = 0
w 30 53 00 
#			# reg[0][0][86] = 32
w 30 56 20 
#			# reg[0][0][87] = 254
w 30 57 fe 
#			# reg[0][0][88] = 0
w 30 58 00 
#			# reg[0][0][89] = 104
w 30 59 68 
#			# reg[0][0][90] = 168
w 30 5a a8 
#			# reg[0][0][91] = 6
w 30 5b 06 
#			# reg[0][0][92] = 0
w 30 5c 00 
#			# reg[0][0][84] = 0
w 30 54 00 
#			# reg[0][0][94] = 32
w 30 5e 20 
#			# reg[0][0][95] = 254
w 30 5f fe 
#			# reg[0][0][96] = 0
w 30 60 00 
#			# reg[0][0][97] = 104
w 30 61 68 
#			# reg[0][0][98] = 168
w 30 62 a8 
#			# reg[0][0][99] = 6
w 30 63 06 
#			# reg[0][0][100] = 0
w 30 64 00 
#			--------------------------------------------------------------- page 4 is selected
w 30 00 04
#			# reg[0][4][118]= 0x06 ; miniDSP_D_in_ter_ch<L3,R3> = ASI3_OUT_CH<L1,R1>
w 30 76 06
#			# reg[  0][  4][ 33] = 0x00	; I2S Format, 16-bit, DOUT2 3-state off
w 30 21 00
#			# reg[  0][  4][ 34] = 0x00	; Offset = 0
w 30 22 00
#			# reg[  0][  4][ 39] = 0x06	; ASI3_in = miniDSP_A OUT3
w 30 27 06
#			# reg[  0][  4][ 40] = 0x50	; miniDSP_D channel mixing
w 30 28 f0
#     #
w 30 2b 01
#     #
w 30 2c 8C
#     #
w 30 2d 20
#     #
w 30 2e 40
#			# reg[  0][  4][ 42] = 0x00	; WCLK3/BCLK3 are ASI3 inputs
w 30 2a 25
#			# reg[  0][  4][ 47] = 0x00	; DOUT3 = ASI3_DOUT
w 30 2f 00
#     #
w 30 49 04
#     #
w 30 4a 04
#			# reg[  0][  4][ 75] = 0x22	; DOUT3 pin enabled, used for ASI3_DOUT
w 30 4b 02
#			# reg[  0][  4][ 76] = 0x20	; DIN3 pin enabled, used for ASI3_DIN
w 30 4c 20
